Scrape All Apps from System Admin (2026-04-12)
====================================
Why: Cron only processes 36 tracked Shopify apps; 13,538 untracked discovered apps
have never had details scraped. User wants a manual "scrape all" trigger with resume
support so partial failures don't waste hours re-scraping fresh apps.

Design:
- New ScraperJobOptions.scope: "tracked" | "all". Default tracked.
- process-job.ts: scope=all routes to AppDetailsScraper.scrapeAll() (method existed,
  wasn't wired). 6h timeout via JOB_TIMEOUT_APP_DETAILS_ALL_MS.
- Admin API /scraper/trigger: force was hardcoded true → now override-able via
  options.force. Tracked default keeps force=true; scope=all UI passes force=false
  to enable 12h cache (resume).
- scrapeAll() writes scrape_runs metadata every 25 apps (items_scraped, total_apps,
  currently_processing, scope:"all") for progress visibility.
- Dashboard: Database icon button in Operational Matrix actions column. Two
  window.confirm() prompts: resume-or-cancel, then force-vs-resume-mode.

Production baseline (2026-04-12): 13,574 Shopify apps; 36 tracked; 2,349 with ≥1
snapshot. Tracked run ~1.4-4.5 apps/sec. Expected full scrape: 1.5-3h.

Resume: existing 12h cache in scrapeApp via buildPreFetchedData(force=false). Partial
run → re-trigger → recent apps skipped.

Trigger: System Admin → Scraper → Operational Matrix → per-platform Database icon →
confirm resume mode → confirm force=false → job enqueued.

PLA-996: Fix Shopify category tree — top-level categories missing, subcategories flat

  Hub categories like "Finding products" have no direct apps → filtered out → children orphaned
- Fix: Build tree with ALL categories first, then pruneEmptyLeaves() removes only
  nodes that have no apps AND no children with apps. Parent hub categories preserved.
- Exported buildTree() and pruneEmptyLeaves() for unit testing
- 7 new tests: buildTree hierarchy + orphan handling, pruneEmptyLeaves multi-level pruning

PLA-998: Fix mobile table overflow — tables still extend beyond viewport
- Root cause: main element had overflow-auto which scrolls both X and Y; wide tables
  caused horizontal page scroll instead of scrolling within the table container
- Fix: Changed main from overflow-auto to overflow-y-auto overflow-x-hidden + max-w-full
  This forces horizontal scrolling to happen at individual table containers (overflow-x-auto)
  while preserving vertical page scroll
- The table.tsx and platform-grouped-table.tsx overflow-x-auto remain the scroll points

PLA-997: Fix Audit Report button — URL, icon, sizing

  - V2 passes iconClassName="h-4 w-4" for consistent h-4 w-4 convention
  - V1 keeps default h-5 w-5 (unchanged)

PLA-975: Fix mobile responsiveness for all dashboard tables
- Root cause: <main> element has flex-1 + overflow-auto but lacked min-w-0
  In flexbox, default min-width: auto prevents flex items from shrinking below
  content width — table content expanded main instead of triggering scroll
- Fix: Added min-w-0 to <main> in dashboard-shell.tsx (one-line CSS fix)
- Table component already had overflow-x-auto (added in prior attempt)
- PlatformGroupedTable already had overflow-x-auto on wrapper
- The min-w-0 was the missing piece that enables the overflow scroll chain
- Added regression test: main must have min-w-0 + overflow-auto

PLA-993: Enhance command palette — 5 improvements + 3 bugfixes
- Fix 1: Modal overlap — FIXED race condition. Previous approach set data-command-palette-open
  via useEffect (async), so PlatformSwitcher handler would fire before attribute was set.
  Now sets attribute synchronously inside the keydown handler's setState callback.
- Fix 2: Developer search — FIXED by separating Promise.all into independent try/catch chains.
  Previously one API failure would block the other. Now each search runs independently.
  Also added Array.isArray(data?.developers) guard for safer response handling.
- Fix 3: Platform badge alignment — moved badge inside name container on same row as app name
  (was outside as sibling, causing vertical centering misalignment with rating below)
- Tests: 14 tests (was 11) — added synchronous attribute test, close attribute test, isolated failure test
- Added size prop ("sm" | "default") to PlatformBadgeCell for compact developer badges
- Updated all command palette tests + added 3 new tests (body attribute, developer search, pages hiding)

PLA-994: Fix developers page — table shows empty results
- Root cause: CTE `dev_apps` joined platform_developers to apps by platform (cross join),
  producing millions of intermediate rows that exceeded 30s statement_timeout on db-f1-micro
- Fix: Replaced CTE + cross-join with LATERAL subquery pattern:
  1. Start from `apps` table (filtered by platform when available)
  2. LATERAL subquery fetches latest snapshot's developer name per app (O(1) with index)
  3. JOIN to platform_developers on (platform, name) using unique index
- Applied same fix to admin listing query (/admin/list)
- Previous CTE approach (commit 63fa061a) materialized ALL latest snapshots then cross-joined
  platform_developers × apps per platform — O(devs × apps) intermediate rows per platform
- New approach: O(apps) with indexed lookups — no cross join, no full materialization
- Added 2 tests: empty-platform short-circuit behavior, platforms query parameter

PLA-990: Optimize slow account API endpoints — starred-features + indexes
- starred-features: Added platform filtering (was scanning ALL apps across ALL platforms)
  JSONB expansion now scoped to current platform via INNER JOIN on apps.platform
- Moved tracked/competitor app fetch BEFORE enrichment query (reordered for parallel use)
- Migration 0134: Added DESC indexes for visibility scores + category snapshots
  (existing ASC indexes can't efficiently serve DISTINCT ON + ORDER BY DESC)
- Most proposed indexes from ticket already existed in migrations 0132/0133

PLA-989: compute_app_scores prerequisite check — platform filtering + fallback
- Bug: checkPrerequisites() did not filter by platform — any platform's completed run satisfied the check
- Bug: No fallback to yesterday's data — if today's scraper failed, scores failed entirely
- Fix: Added platform parameter to SQL WHERE clause, matching platform column + idx_scrape_runs_platform_type_started index
- Fix: Added yesterday fallback — if today's run is missing for a type, checks yesterday's completed runs
- Added 6 unit tests for the fallback classification logic
- Error messages now include platform name for easier debugging

PLA-992: Competitor Watch card shows empty state for tracked app with competitors
- Root cause: getAppCompetitors() in api.ts used `&includeChanges=true` instead of `?includeChanges=true`
  This placed the param BEFORE the `?` added by withPlatform(), making it part of the URL path
  Fastify couldn't match the route → 404 → silently caught by .catch(() => [])
- Fix: Changed `&` to `?` in params construction
- Also added error logging to .catch() in page.tsx so API errors are no longer silent
- Added 2 regression tests in api.test.ts verifying URL construction with includeChanges+platform

Keywords API Performance Optimization (2026-04-10)
===================================================

PLA-983: Optimize GET /api/keywords — response time >3s

Changes:
1. Parallelized Query 1 (tracked keywords) with Query 2 (tracked/competitor apps) using Promise.all
2. Pushed JSONB filtering into SQL — instead of transferring full results blob (10KB-100KB+),
   only extract matched app slugs via jsonb_array_elements subquery
3. Converted Array.includes() to Set.has() for O(1) slug lookups
4. Used platform-filtered keyword IDs for downstream queries (ads, tags, snapshots)
5. Parallelized ad counts, tag fetching, and snapshot queries into a single Promise.all
6. Skipped migration — idx_account_tracked_keywords_account already exists (migration 0110)

Files changed:
- apps/api/src/routes/keywords.ts (GET / handler rewritten)
- apps/api/src/__tests__/routes/keywords.test.ts (+3 Set-based filtering tests)

PLA-984: Fix Salesforce platform page slow API responses (7-10s per endpoint)

Changes:
1. Migration 0133: Added two CONCURRENTLY indexes:
   - idx_notifications_user_read_archived ON notifications (user_id, is_read, is_archived) — covers unread-count filter
   - idx_app_cat_rankings_app_cat_scraped ON app_category_rankings (app_id, category_slug, scraped_at DESC) — covers competitors windowed queries
2. Skipped indexes for app_visibility_scores and app_power_scores — already well-indexed
3. Skipped notifications user_id index — already exists as idx_notifications_user_unread
4. Auth/me already optimized (consolidated to single round-trip)

PLA-982: Optimize GET /api/account/starred-categories — parallelize initial queries

Changes:
1. Parallelized starred rows + tracked apps + competitor apps into single Promise.all
   (was: starred rows → then [tracked, competitor] in parallel = 2 round-trips, now 1)

PLA-981: Fix featured label readability

PLA-979: Optimize GET /api/developers — correlated subqueries cause 1s+ response time

Changes:
1. Rewrote main developers query to use CTEs instead of correlated subqueries:
   - latest_snapshots CTE: DISTINCT ON (app_id) computed once, not per row
   - dev_apps CTE: joins platform_developers + apps + latest_snapshots once
   - dev_app_counts CTE: aggregates app counts from dev_apps
   - dev_top_apps CTE: builds top 5 app icons from dev_apps
2. Added expression index: idx_app_snapshots_developer_name ON app_snapshots((developer->>'name'))
3. Same CTE pattern already used in admin endpoint — consistency fix

Files changed:
- apps/api/src/routes/developers.ts (GET / query rewrite)
- packages/db/src/migrations/0133_salesforce_performance_indexes.sql (added developer name index)

Keywords Page Performance — N+1 Query Elimination (2026-04-10)
================================================================

PLA-978: Fix N+1 queries and connection pool starvation causing 40+ second page loads

Changes:
1. Keywords endpoint (account-tracking.ts): Replace per-keyword snapshot queries in
   Promise.all with single DISTINCT ON batch query. N queries → 1 query.
2. Competitors endpoint (account-tracking.ts): Replace per-competitor snapshot + change
   queries in Promise.all with two batch queries (DISTINCT ON for snapshots, GROUP BY
   for last change dates). 2N queries → 2 queries.
3. Connection pool (index.ts): Increase max from 5 → 10 (Cloud SQL allows 25).
   Also updated pool reset to match.
4. Cross-platform keywords (cross-platform.ts): Replace LATERAL JOIN with
   DISTINCT ON subquery + regular LEFT JOIN for latest keyword snapshots.
5. V2 app page (page.tsx): Eliminate waterfall — competitors/keywords fetched in
   parallel with all other data instead of waiting for Round 1 to complete.

Impact: Keywords page should load in 2-5s instead of 40+. All endpoints benefit
from doubled connection pool capacity.

Auth Refresh/Logout Validation Fix (2026-04-10)
================================================================

Fix: POST /api/auth/refresh and /api/auth/logout crash with 500 when refreshToken is missing
- Root cause: Zod .parse() throws uncaught ZodError when body is empty/invalid
- Fix: Changed to .safeParse() with explicit 401/400 response
- Impact: Prevents infinite refresh loop when token expires or cookie is cleared

================================================================

PLA-962: Fix Zoho keyword scraper timeout — page.content() hangs after search page load

Fix Developers Page Sorting by Apps Column (2026-04-09)
================================================================

PLA-923: Fix broken sorting on developers listing pages — sorting by Apps column didn't work
- Root cause: drizzle-orm sql`app_count` parameterized the column name as a string value
  instead of treating it as a SQL identifier. The ORDER BY was sorting by the literal string
  'app_count' instead of the app_count column.
- Fix: replaced sql`app_count` with sql.raw() for the ORDER BY clause

Fix Excessive Stale Scraper Jobs (2026-04-09)
================================================================

PLA-959: Investigate and fix excessive stale jobs for App Details and Keywords scrapers
- Root cause analysis: 3 contributing factors identified:
  1. BullMQ default lockDuration (30s) too short for 30-45 min scraper jobs — event loop
     delays during browser scraping cause false "stalled" detection
  2. Retry tracking was broken — meta.retryOf was never stored in scrape_run metadata,
     so the retry guard never triggered (retryOf from job data didn't flow through)
  3. MAX_RETRIES=1 too low for Spot VM preemption recovery
- Fixes applied:
  - Added BULLMQ_LOCK_DURATION_MS (5 min) and BULLMQ_STALLED_INTERVAL_MS (5 min) to
    both background and interactive workers — locks renew every 2.5 min
  - Replaced broken meta.retryOf check with DB-based retry counting: queries recent
    stale-run-retry scrape_runs per platform+type in 6-hour window
  - Increased MAX_RETRIES from 1 to 3
  - Retry count tracked within cleanup cycle (prevents exceeding limit in single pass)
- Files changed:
  - apps/scraper/src/constants.ts (new constants)
  - apps/scraper/src/worker.ts (lockDuration, stalledInterval on both workers)
  - apps/scraper/src/jobs/cleanup-stale-runs.ts (retry logic rewrite)
  - apps/scraper/src/__tests__/jobs/cleanup-stale-runs.test.ts (7 tests)

BrowserClient OOM Crash Recovery (2026-04-07)
================================================================

PLA-864: Fix Salesforce app_details scraper browser crash (OOM recovery)
- Problem: When Playwright browser crashes mid-scrape (OOM on Spot VM), subsequent fetches fail
  with "Target page, context or browser has been closed" — BrowserClient didn't detect or recover
- Solution:
  - Added `recycleBrowser()` to BrowserPool — forcefully closes crashed browser and resets state
    so next `getBrowser()` launches fresh instance
  - Added crash detection in BrowserClient via `isBrowserCrash()` static method — matches 5 error
    patterns: "Target page, context or browser has been closed", "browser has been closed",
    "Browser closed", "Protocol error", "Target closed"
  - Wrapped both `fetchPage()` and `withPage()` with try/catch — on crash, recycle browser and
    retry ONCE with fresh context
  - Also made context.close() calls use `.catch(() => {})` in finally blocks since context may
    already be dead after crash
- Files changed: browser-client.ts, browser-pool.ts
- Tests: 18 new tests (14 browser-client + 4 browser-pool recycleBrowser)

Date Serialization in SQL Templates — Remaining Fixes (2026-04-07)
================================================================

PLA-867: Fix remaining raw Date objects in sql tagged template literals
- Prior commits (0042bf77, 47bacd8c) fixed sql templates in bounce-handler, eligibility,
  event-dispatcher, suppression, notification-stream
- This fix covers 13 remaining locations across 5 files where `const cutoff = new Date()`
  was interpolated into sql`` templates without .toISOString()
- Affected files: email-analytics.ts (4), email-errors.ts (3), notification-analytics.ts (3),
  email-alerts.ts (1), admin-notifications.ts (1)
- Root cause: Buffer.byteLength() in postgres-js driver rejects Date objects in sql template
  interpolation — must be ISO strings. Note: Drizzle .set()/.values() handle Date objects fine.
- Added regression test (sql-date-serialization.test.ts) that scans source files for raw Date
  objects in sql templates to prevent future regressions

Zendesk Review Scraper — Switch to REST API (2026-04-07)
================================================================

PLA-866: Fix Zendesk review scraper failure
- Root cause: CSS selectors in review-parser.ts were speculative and never matched
  real Zendesk DOM (React SPA behind Cloudflare). Browser scraping yielded 0 reviews.
- Solution: Switched from BrowserClient (Playwright) to Zendesk Marketplace REST API v2:
  `marketplace.zendesk.com/api/v2/apps/{numericId}/reviews.json`
- API returns: id, rating (1-5), review text, created_at, user_details.name
- Pagination via next_url (since_id cursor-based), 5 reviews per page
- No Cloudflare blocking on the API endpoint
- Eliminated browser overhead entirely for review scraping
- Updated: review-parser.ts (JSON parsing), index.ts (API fetch), urls.ts (API URL)
- 11 new tests replacing 7 old tests (now testing JSON API response parsing)

DB Pool Reliability — Active Recovery & Hardening (2026-04-07)
================================================================

Root cause: postgres.js connection pool periodically gets stuck (all connections drop to 0).
DB is reachable via healthDb but main pool can't create new connections.
Triggered by Cloud SQL maintenance/network blips + aggressive idle_timeout (20s) + no keep-alive.

PLA-841: Active pool recovery
- On 3rd consecutive health check failure, reset pool (close old, create new) instead of waiting for process.exit
- resetPool() creates new pool first, verifies it works, then swaps + closes old in background
- Exit threshold raised from 5 to 7 failures (gives recovery time after reset attempt)
- New metrics: db_pool_resets gauge tracks total resets since process start

PLA-842: Pool config tuning
- idle_timeout: 20s → 60s (prevents premature connection death during low traffic)
- keep_alive: 30s (TCP keepalive detects dead connections before queries fail)
- max_lifetime jitter: ±25% randomization prevents thundering herd (all connections dying at once)
- Exported closeDb() utility for pool reset

PLA-843: Docker healthcheck uses /health/ready
- Changed from /health (always 200 via healthDb) to /health/ready (returns 503 when pool stuck)
- timeout: 5s → 10s, start_period: 30s → 45s (account for pool init time)
- Updated both docker-compose-api.yml and docker-compose.prod.yml

PLA-844: Connection warming (60s interval)
- Periodic SELECT 1 through main pool keeps at least 1 connection alive
- Runs independently of traffic — prevents all connections from idling out during low-traffic periods
- Failures logged but don't increment pool monitor counter (avoids double-counting)

PLA-845: External uptime monitoring docs
- Added Section 5.3 to SYSTEM_ARCHITECTURE.md with UptimeRobot setup instructions
- Monitors: /health/ready + dashboard, 5-min interval, alert on 2 consecutive failures

PLA-846: Request-level retry middleware
- GET requests automatically retry once (500ms delay) on transient DB errors
- Detects: ECONNREFUSED, ECONNRESET, connection terminated, PG codes 57P01/57P03/08006/08001/08004
- Non-idempotent requests (POST/PUT/DELETE) never retried
- Response includes x-db-retry header for observability
- 14 unit tests for isTransientDbError()

PLA-847: DB proxy for pool reset propagation
- Route handlers capture `const db = app.db` at registration time
- After pool reset, these closures still pointed to old dead pool
- Fix: Proxy object delegates all method calls to current `db` reference
- `app.decorate("db", dbProxy)` — routes capture proxy, proxy forwards to latest pool
- Zero changes to 51 route files — fully transparent

PLA-849: Fix healthcheck pg_settings access on Cloud SQL
- Cloud SQL restricts `pg_settings` table access
- Changed from subquery `(SELECT setting::int FROM pg_settings)` to `SHOW max_connections`
- Fallback to 25 (db-f1-micro default) if SHOW fails

PLA-851: Connection exhaustion fix — pool size reduction
- Cloud SQL db-f1-micro max_connections=25, was being exceeded
- API: max 10 → 5, email workers: 10 → 2 each, notification worker: 10 → 2, scheduler: 10 → 2
- New total: API(5) + healthDb(1) + worker(5) + cli(3) + email(2+2) + notification(2) + scheduler(2) = 22
- resetPool() now checks connection headroom before creating new pool
- If near limit (>=20), closes old pool first before creating new one

PLA-852: Fix empty IN() clause with research-mode keywords
- `apps/api/src/routes/apps.ts` line 109: keyword batch query generated `IN ()` SQL syntax error
- Occurred when account has only research-mode keywords (trackedAppId=null)
- Added guard: skip ranked keyword query when allTrackedAppIds is empty

PLA-848: Cloud SQL connection drops at ~26 min (resolved by PLA-851)
- Root cause was connection exhaustion (25 limit) not GCP proxy timeout
- All fixes combined (reduced pools, recovery, warming, retry) prevent recurrence

PLA-850: skip_reason column error (not from app code)
- Cloud SQL error log referenced el.skip_reason which doesn't exist in schema
- Confirmed: no application code references this column
- Likely a manual SQL query — monitor for recurrence

DB Pool Fix — Connection Reduction (2026-04-07)
================================================================

PLA-822: Phase 2: Consolidate /api/system-admin/accounts N+1 into single query
- Replaced N+1 pattern (7 queries per account × N accounts) with single SQL using correlated subselects
- 10 accounts: 70+ queries → 2 queries (accounts+counts + packages)

PLA-821: Phase 1: Consolidate /api/auth/me from 9 parallel queries to 1+2
- Replaced 9-query Promise.all with single SQL query using scalar subselects for 6 COUNTs
- Account data + usage counts fetched in 1 round-trip (was 7 separate queries)
- accountPlatforms + platformVisibility remain as 2 parallel queries
- 9 connections per request → 3 connections (67% reduction)
- Updated auth tests and critical-flows test with executeResult mock

Performance Optimization: Dashboard Page Load (2026-04-05)
================================================================

Problem: Login sonrası ve platform sayfaları çok yavaş yükleniyor.

Root causes:
1. /api/overview/highlights 8 sequential DB sorgusu yapıyor (toplam 2-5 saniye)
2. keyword/category movers CTE'leri correlated subquery kullanıyor (O(n²))
3. Overview highlights "non-blocking" görünüyor ama aslında await ile bekleniyor
4. Platform sayfasında categories fetch apps yüklendikten sonra sequential

Fixes:
1. highlights: 8 sequential → Promise.all ile 7 parallel + 1 dependent = ~70% hızlanma
2. keyword movers: DISTINCT ON + correlated subquery → ROW_NUMBER() window function
3. category movers: Aynı pattern, window function ile değiştirildi
4. Overview: highlights fetch'i truly non-blocking (fire-and-forget, setDataLoaded önce)
5. Platform page: categories fetch non-blocking (fire-and-forget after setLoading(false))

PLA-453: AI competitor suggestion API endpoints (2026-03-30)
================================================================
Modified GET /api/account/tracked-apps/:slug/competitor-suggestions:
- Added ?source=all|jaccard|ai query parameter (default: all)
- Added aiStatus and aiGeneratedAt fields
- source=ai returns cached AI merged results
- source=all returns AI if cached, falls back to Jaccard

Added POST /api/account/tracked-apps/:slug/ai-competitor-suggestions/generate:
- Cache check → candidate collection → AI call → merge → store → return
- Collects Jaccard top 48 candidates from category rankings
- preFilterCandidates compresses to top 60 with 5 features each
- generateCompetitorSuggestions with 6-dimension evaluation
- mergeCompetitorScores: 0.6 × AI + 0.4 × Jaccard
- 7-day cache TTL, concurrent generation protection
- Logs to ai_logs

PLA-452: AI keyword suggestion API endpoints (2026-03-30)
================================================================
Modified GET /api/account/tracked-apps/:slug/keyword-suggestions:
- Added ?source=all|ngram|ai query parameter (default: all)
  - all: returns AI merged if cached, falls back to n-gram
  - ngram: original behavior (n-gram only)
  - ai: AI results only (from cache)
- Added aiStatus field: available | generating | expired | not_generated
- Added aiGeneratedAt field

Added POST /api/account/tracked-apps/:slug/ai-keyword-suggestions/generate:
- Checks cache first — returns if valid and not expired
- 409 if already generating
- Collects context: snapshot, tracked keywords, n-gram top 20
- Calls generateKeywordSuggestions (gpt-4o-mini)
- Merges AI + n-gram via mergeKeywords (50 max)
- Stores in ai_keyword_suggestions cache (7-day TTL)
- Logs to ai_logs
- Error handling: timeout, rate limit, quota

Also fixed: ai_suggestion tables app_id changed from UUID to INTEGER (apps.id is serial)

PLA-450: AI competitor suggestion engine (2026-03-30)
================================================================
Created packages/shared/src/ai-competitor-suggestions.ts implementing AI competitive
intelligence with 6 evaluation dimensions:
- Value Proposition Overlap (30%), Target Audience Match (20%), Feature Functionality
  Overlap (20%), Market Positioning (15%), Keyword/Search Overlap (10%),
  Category Proximity (5%)
- Competitor classification: direct, indirect, alternative, aspirational
- Hybrid scoring: finalScore = 0.6 × AI + 0.4 × Jaccard × 100
- Flags: "semantic_competitor" (AI>70, Jaccard<0.1), "superficially_similar" (Jaccard>0.5, AI<30)
- preFilterCandidates: Jaccard top 48 + sightings, cap at 60, compress features to top 5
- 20 unit tests covering filtering, input building, score merging, normalization

PLA-449: AI keyword suggestion engine (2026-03-30)
================================================================
Created packages/shared/src/ai-keyword-suggestions.ts implementing an ASO-inspired
5-tier keyword suggestion engine:

- ASO Weight Model: App Title (10x), Subtitle (7x), Introduction (5x), Features (4x),
  Categories (3x), Description (2x), Pricing Plans (1x), Developer (0.5x)
- 5-Tier Keyword Model: Direct Match (90-100), Feature Keywords (70-89), Problem/Intent
  (50-69), Adjacent/Semantic (30-49), Long-tail Opportunities (10-29)
- buildKeywordSuggestionInput() — collects app metadata + context into prompt format
- generateKeywordSuggestions() — calls AI with ASO system prompt, validates/clamps output
- mergeKeywords() — hybrid scoring combining AI + n-gram results:
  - Both AI + n-gram → 20% score boost (capped at 100)
  - N-gram only → normalized to 0-80 range, assigned tier 2
  - AI only → original score
- Uses gpt-4o-mini by default (cheaper for keyword generation)
- JSON schema validation for structured output
- 27 unit tests covering input building, response parsing, score merging, normalization

PLA-448: Shared AI service layer (2026-03-30)
================================================================
Created packages/shared/src/ai-service.ts with:
- computeCost(model, promptTokens, completionTokens) — model pricing table for 8 models
- callAI(options) — wraps OpenAI call with retry logic, timing, cost calculation, JSON parsing
  Uses dependency injection (AIClient interface) so shared doesn't depend on openai package
- logAICall(db, aiLogsTable, params) — inserts into ai_logs, silently catches errors
  Uses DI for db and table reference so shared doesn't depend on @appranks/db
- isRateLimitOrQuota(err) — detects 429/quota errors for caller error handling

Refactored apps/api/src/routes/research.ts to use callAI + logAICall instead of
inline OpenAI calls. No behavior change — same model, temperature, timeout, prompts.

21 unit tests covering cost calculation, retry logic, response parsing, error handling,
and logging.

PLA-458: Fix duplicate key constraint error in non-Shopify category scraper (2026-03-30)
================================================================
Root cause: `recordNormalizedAppRankings` in category-scraper.ts (used by all non-Shopify
platforms) was missing `.onConflictDoNothing()` on the `appCategoryRankings` insert.
The Shopify path (`recordAppRankings`) already had it. When the same app appeared in
multiple pages or overlapping scrape runs on the same day, the unique index
`idx_app_cat_rank_daily_unique` on `(app_id, category_slug, DATE(scraped_at))` raised
a duplicate key violation.

Fix: Added `.onConflictDoNothing()` to the insert at line ~948, matching the Shopify path.
This is a one-line fix that protects all non-Shopify platforms (Salesforce, Canva, Wix,
WordPress, Google Workspace, Atlassian, Zoom, Zoho, Zendesk, HubSpot).

Tests: 3 new tests in category-scraper-rankings.test.ts verifying onConflictDoNothing
is called, duplicate inserts don't throw, and sponsored apps are skipped.

Email & Notification Infrastructure: Phase 0 (2026-03-30)
================================================================
PLA-415: Added 3 new BullMQ queues (email-instant, email-bulk, notifications)
in queue.ts with distinct retry/backoff configs:
- email-instant: 3 retries, 5s exponential backoff (transactional, <30s SLA)
- email-bulk: 2 retries, 30s exponential backoff (marketing/digest)
- notifications: 3 retries, 10s exponential backoff (in-app + push)
Shared types: InstantEmailJobData, BulkEmailJobData, NotificationJobData
in packages/shared/src/types/email-job.ts and notification-job.ts.

- No tracking pixel, no unsubscribe link (transactional exemption)
- Uses existing design tokens and components (layout, header, ctaButton)

PLA-416: Implemented email-instant worker (email-instant-worker.ts).
- Processes jobs from email-instant queue with concurrency: 3
- Routes to template → renders HTML → logs to email_logs → sends via SMTP
- Failed jobs after 3 attempts go to dead_letter_jobs table
- Core logic extracted to email/process-instant-email.ts for testability

PLA-419: Implemented email-bulk worker (email-bulk-worker.ts).
- Processes marketing/digest email jobs from email-bulk queue
- Concurrency: 5, rate limit: 50 jobs/min via BullMQ limiter
- Routes to existing template builders (digest, weekly, ranking alert, etc.)
- Uses full 6-step pipeline: eligibility → unsubscribe → log → track → send
- Core logic in email/process-bulk-email.ts for testability

PLA-420: Implemented notification worker (notification-worker.ts).
- Processes notification jobs from notifications queue
- Concurrency: 5, rate limit: 100 jobs/min
- Creates NotificationStore implementation backed by Drizzle
- Uses shared emitNotification engine (eligibility, dedup, rate limit)
- Optional web push via VAPID (dynamic import of web-push)
- Push failures handled: 410/404 → deactivate, 5 failures → deactivate
- Delivery logged to notification_delivery_log table

PLA-421: Event detector module (apps/scraper/src/events/event-detector.ts).
6 detection functions: checkRankingAlerts, checkCategoryAlerts,
checkCompetitorMoves, checkNewReviews, detectMilestones, checkFeaturedChanges.
Configurable thresholds (DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS). Returns DetectedEvent[] with
type, appId, platform, severity, data. 28 unit tests.

PLA-422: Event dispatcher (apps/scraper/src/events/event-dispatcher.ts).
dispatch() finds affected users via accountTrackedApps + accountCompetitorApps,
enqueues to email-bulk and notifications queues. EMAIL_EVENT_TYPES controls
which events generate emails vs notification-only. dispatchAll() for batches.

PLA-423: Integrated event detection into process-job.ts.
afterKeywordScrape() after keyword_search, afterCategoryScrape() after category.
All wrapped in try/catch — event detection never breaks scraping.

CORS Handling for API Unavailability: PLA-410 (2026-03-29)
================================================================
Problem: When API is down, Traefik returns 502/503/504 without CORS headers.
Browser blocks the response entirely (TypeError: Failed to fetch), hiding the
real error behind a confusing CORS message.

Dashboard-side fix:
- auth-context.tsx doFetch: catch network errors → return synthetic 503 Response
- lib/api.ts fetchApi/fetchPublicApi: catch network errors → throw user-friendly error
- Callers now see "Service temporarily unavailable" instead of opaque TypeError

TODO (server-side): Add CORS middleware to Traefik via Coolify dashboard so
error responses also include Access-Control-Allow-Origin headers.

Fix DB Pool Hang: PLA-409 (2026-03-29)
================================================================
Problem: postgres.js connection pool enters stuck state after concurrent
query bursts. All requests (including /health) hang indefinitely.
Pool believes connections are "in use" but they're closed at DB level.

Solution:
- Reduced pool max from 20 to 10 (single Node.js process doesn't need 20)
- Added statement_timeout: 30s to prevent queries from hanging forever
- Created separate health check DB client (max: 1, 5s timeout) so /health
  never blocks when main pool is stuck
- /health/ready now also probes main pool with 5s timeout to detect stuck state
- Added pool health monitor (every 30s) that logs warnings + sets Prometheus
  gauge (db_pool_stuck) when pool can't respond
- Coolify health check (hitting /health) will detect degraded state and
  restart the container automatically

Eliminate N+1 Query Patterns in API Routes (2026-03-29)
================================================================

2. categories.ts GET /:slug children: Per-child appCount fetch → DISTINCT ON batch

3 endpoints were already fixed in prior work (apps.ts GET /, account-extras.ts, keywords.ts GET /).
Added 3 new tests for POST /opportunity endpoint.

Fix SQL Errors Causing 500s on Homepage /api/apps Endpoint (2026-03-29)
================================================================
**PLA-236:** Two separate SQL bugs causing 500 errors across multiple platforms.

- Bug 1: Empty IN() clause when account has tracked apps for other platforms but
  none for the requested platform. Added early return when appIds2 is empty.
- Bug 2: category_snapshots query used non-existent column "category_slug".
  Fixed by joining with categories table and using category_id.
- Added regression test for empty platform case.

Implement Circuit Breaker Pattern for Platform Scraper Failures (2026-03-28)
=============================================================================
**PLA-199:** Prevent wasted scraping when a platform is down/blocking.

**Implementation:**
1. **`apps/scraper/src/circuit-breaker.ts`** — Redis-backed circuit breaker:
   - 3 states: CLOSED (normal), OPEN (paused), HALF-OPEN (testing)
   - Opens after 5 consecutive failures (configurable: CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD)
   - Stays open for 1h (configurable: CIRCUIT_BREAKER_OPEN_DURATION_MS)
   - Transitions to half-open after pause; success closes, failure re-opens
   - Fail-open: if Redis unavailable, all circuits allow requests
2. **Scheduler integration** — checks `isCircuitOpen()` before enqueuing jobs
3. **Worker integration** — `recordSuccess()`/`recordFailure()` after each job
4. **Admin API:**
   - `GET /api/system-admin/circuit-breakers` — list all circuit states
   - `POST /api/system-admin/circuit-breakers/:platform/override` — force state

**Files changed:**
- `apps/scraper/src/circuit-breaker.ts` (new)
- `apps/scraper/src/scheduler.ts` — circuit check before enqueue
- `apps/scraper/src/process-job.ts` — recordSuccess/recordFailure
- `apps/api/src/routes/system-admin.ts` — admin circuit breaker endpoints
- `apps/scraper/src/__tests__/circuit-breaker.test.ts` (new, 9 tests)
- `files/RISK_ANALYSIS_V3.md` — R-01 updated

Implement Browser Connection Pooling for Scraper Worker (2026-03-28)
=====================================================================
**PLA-187:** Prevent OOM kills by reusing a single Chromium process across jobs.

**Implementation:**
1. **`apps/scraper/src/browser-pool.ts`** — Singleton `BrowserPool`:
   - Single Chromium process shared across all jobs
   - Each job gets isolated `BrowserContext` (cookies/storage)
   - Auto-recycles after 10 jobs or 1 hour (env: BROWSER_POOL_MAX_JOBS, BROWSER_POOL_MAX_LIFETIME_MS)
   - Thread-safe: concurrent `getBrowser()` calls wait for same launch promise
   - `getStats()` for monitoring (jobCount, uptime, isConnected)
2. **`browser-client.ts`** refactored to use pool instead of launching own browser
3. **Graceful shutdown** — `onCleanup` callback in `createGracefulShutdown`; worker closes pool on SIGTERM/SIGINT

**Files changed:**
- `apps/scraper/src/browser-pool.ts` (new)
- `apps/scraper/src/browser-client.ts` — uses browserPool instead of own chromium.launch
- `apps/scraper/src/worker.ts` — imports browserPool, passes onCleanup to shutdown
- `apps/scraper/src/graceful-shutdown.ts` — added onCleanup option
- `apps/scraper/src/__tests__/browser-pool.test.ts` (new, 7 tests)
- `files/RISK_ANALYSIS_V3.md` — R-03 marked as Mitigated

Implement Data Retention and Cleanup Job (2026-03-28)
=====================================================
**PLA-191:** Prevent unbounded database growth from snapshot tables.

**Implementation:**
1. **`apps/scraper/src/jobs/data-cleanup.ts`** — New cleanup job:
   - Deletes old rows from app_snapshots, keyword_snapshots, scrape_runs, dead_letter_jobs
   - Configurable retention via env vars (DATA_RETENTION_SNAPSHOT_MONTHS=12, etc.)
   - Runs VACUUM ANALYZE after each table cleanup
   - Graceful: continues with remaining tables if one fails

3. **Job type** `data_cleanup` added to ScraperJobType, process-job switch, admin trigger

**Default retention:** snapshots 12mo, scrape_runs 6mo, DLQ 3mo

Implement Redis-Backed Access Token Blacklist (2026-03-28)
============================================================
**PLA-194:** Enable immediate access token revocation before 15-min expiry.

**Implementation:**
1. **`jti` claim** added to all access tokens via `crypto.randomUUID()` in `generateAccessToken()`
2. **`apps/api/src/utils/token-blacklist.ts`** — Redis-backed blacklist:
   - `blacklistToken(jti, expiresAt)` — stores jti with TTL = remaining token lifetime
   - `isTokenBlacklisted(jti)` — O(1) Redis GET check
   - `revokeAllTokensForUser(userId)` — stores "revoked-before" timestamp (900s TTL)
   - `isUserTokenRevoked(userId, iat)` — compares token iat vs revocation time
   - Fail-open: if Redis unavailable, all checks return false
3. **Auth middleware** updated to check both jti blacklist and user-level revocation
4. **Logout** (`POST /api/auth/logout`) now blacklists the current access token
5. **New endpoint** `POST /api/auth/revoke-all-sessions`:
   - Invalidates all access tokens for the user (revoke-before timestamp)
   - Deletes all refresh tokens from DB

**Files changed:**
- `apps/api/src/middleware/auth.ts` — added jti to JwtPayload, blacklist checks
- `apps/api/src/routes/auth.ts` — jti in token, blacklist on logout, revoke-all endpoint
- `apps/api/src/utils/token-blacklist.ts` (new)
- `apps/api/src/__tests__/utils/token-blacklist.test.ts` (new, 8 tests)
- `files/RISK_ANALYSIS_V3.md` — R-21 marked as Mitigated

Add Idempotency Keys to Critical POST Endpoints (2026-03-28)
==============================================================
**PLA-197:** Prevent duplicate operations from network retries or double-clicks.

**Implementation:**
1. **`apps/api/src/middleware/idempotency.ts`** — Two exports:
   - `requireIdempotencyKey()` — preHandler hook that checks `Idempotency-Key` header.
     If cached response exists → replay with `x-idempotency-replayed: true`.
     If "processing" → 409 Conflict. Otherwise marks as processing.
   - `registerIdempotencyOnSend()` — global onSend hook that caches 2xx responses and
     clears processing markers on failures (so the key can be retried).
2. **Redis-backed storage** with 24h TTL. Keys scoped by accountId to prevent cross-account collisions.
3. **Graceful degradation** — if Redis is unavailable, requests proceed without idempotency.

**Protected endpoints:**
- POST /api/research-projects (research.ts)
- POST /api/account/tracked-apps (account-tracking.ts)
- POST /api/account/members (account-members.ts)
- POST /api/system-admin/scraper/trigger (system-admin.ts)

**Files changed:**
- `apps/api/src/middleware/idempotency.ts` (new)
- `apps/api/src/constants.ts` — added `IDEMPOTENCY_TTL_SECONDS`
- `apps/api/src/index.ts` — registered global onSend hook
- 4 route files — added `requireIdempotencyKey()` to preHandler
- `apps/api/src/__tests__/middleware/idempotency.test.ts` (new, 8 tests)
- `files/RISK_ANALYSIS_V3.md` — R-74 marked as Mitigated

Fix Middleware Blocking Cross-Platform Pages (2026-03-28)
=========================================================
**PLA-221:** The middleware in `proxy.ts` was redirecting `/apps`, `/keywords`, `/competitors`
to `/shopify/apps`, `/shopify/keywords`, `/shopify/competitors` — blocking cross-platform pages.

**Root cause:** The legacy redirect matched any path starting with a PLATFORM_PAGES entry where
the first segment wasn't a valid platform. Since "apps", "keywords", "competitors" aren't platforms,
bare paths like `/apps` were incorrectly redirected.

**Fix:** Added `CROSS_PLATFORM_PAGES` exclusion list. Exact matches for `/apps`, `/keywords`,
`/competitors` now pass through to the cross-platform page components. Paths with additional
segments (e.g., `/apps/some-slug`) still redirect to `/shopify/apps/some-slug` for backward compat.

**Files changed:**
- `apps/dashboard/src/proxy.ts` — added CROSS_PLATFORM_PAGES array, added exclusion check
- `apps/dashboard/src/__tests__/middleware.test.ts` — 5 new tests for cross-platform pages
- `apps/dashboard/src/__tests__/lib/proxy.test.ts` — updated existing test + added legacy path test

Adopt TanStack Query for Dashboard Data Fetching (2026-03-28)
=============================================================
**PLA-146:** Set up TanStack Query (React Query v5) infrastructure and converted 2 key pages
as foundational examples for incremental migration.

**Infrastructure created:**
1. **`@tanstack/react-query` v5.75.0** added to dashboard dependencies
2. **`apps/dashboard/src/lib/query-client.ts`** — QueryClient factory with sensible defaults
   (staleTime: 30s, retry: 1, refetchOnWindowFocus: false). Browser singleton pattern to
   avoid cross-request leaks on SSR.
3. **`apps/dashboard/src/components/providers.tsx`** — Client component wrapping children with
   `QueryClientProvider`. Integrated into root layout.tsx (wraps AuthProvider).
4. **`apps/dashboard/src/lib/use-api-query.ts`** — Two typed hooks:
   - `useApiQuery<T>(key, url, options?)` — wraps `useQuery` + `fetchWithAuth`, handles error
     parsing, returns typed data.
   - `useApiMutation<TResponse, TBody>(url, fetchOptions?, mutationOptions?)` — wraps
     `useMutation` + `fetchWithAuth` for POST/PUT/DELETE operations.
   - Re-exports `useQueryClient` for convenience.

**Pages converted (2 examples):**
1. **`[platform]/apps/page.tsx`** — Replaced manual `useState/useEffect/fetchWithAuth` with
   `useApiQuery`. Apps list fetched via `["apps", platform]` key. Categories fetched with
   custom `queryFn` (POST body). Track/untrack use `invalidateQueries` instead of manual reload.
2. **`[platform]/categories/page.tsx`** — Two parallel queries: categories (tree or flat format)
   and starred categories. Star/unstar mutations invalidate starred query cache.

**Tests added:**
- `src/__tests__/lib/use-api-query.test.tsx` — 8 tests covering: successful fetch, API error
  handling, error with no body, enabled option, multiple queries, mutation request, mutation
  error, onSuccess callback.
- Updated `apps-list.test.tsx` and `categories-list.test.tsx` to mock `@/lib/use-api-query`
  instead of testing against raw `fetchWithAuth` calls.

**Migration pattern for remaining pages:**
Replace `useState + useEffect + fetchWithAuth` with `useApiQuery(key, url)`. For mutations,
use `useApiMutation` or call `fetchWithAuth` directly then `queryClient.invalidateQueries()`.
All 1284 tests passing.

Eliminate `any` Type Casts & Zod Request Validation (2026-03-28)
==============================================================
**PLA-141:** Removed request-body `any` casts across the API and strengthened Zod validation.

**Key changes:**
1. **Fastify `db` type augmentation** — Created `apps/api/src/types/fastify.d.ts` that
   augments `FastifyInstance` with a typed `db` property. This eliminates `(app as any).db`
   casts across **25 files** (22 route files, 1 middleware, 1 test helper, 1 index).
2. **Removed 16 local `type Db = ReturnType<typeof createDb>` aliases** — no longer
   needed since the type is declared globally via module augmentation.
3. **Removed unused `createDb` imports** from 16 route files that only imported it for
   the `Db` type alias.
4. **Fixed `(request.query as any)` casts** in platform-attributes.ts, integrations.ts,
   and account-tracking.ts — replaced with properly typed `Querystring` generics.
5. **Fixed `(request as any).user` casts** in system-admin.ts (4 occurrences) — `request.user`
   is already typed via the existing Fastify module augmentation in auth middleware.
6. **Typed error handler** in index.ts — replaced `error: any` with `Error & { statusCode?: number }`,
   added proper `ZodError` type assertion.
7. **Improved research schema** — replaced `z.any()` for `categories` and `pricingPlans`
   with `z.array(z.record(z.string(), z.unknown()))` to reject non-object array items.
8. **Fixed `getPlatformFromQuery` utility** — removed `as any` cast, uses `query?.platform as string`.

**New test files (1 file):**
- `apps/api/src/__tests__/types/fastify-db.test.ts` — 1 test verifying `app.db` is
  accessible with proper typing in route handlers (select/insert/update/delete/execute).

**Updated tests:**
- `apps/api/src/__tests__/schemas/research.test.ts` — 4 new tests for categories/pricingPlans
  schema validation (accepts record objects, rejects primitives).

**Impact:** 25+ files have cleaner types. All 748 API tests pass. The `(app as any).db`
pattern (previously the #1 source of `any` casts) is completely eliminated.

   in 13 parser files across all platforms. Returns null instead of NaN.

   in process-job.ts (3 cascade loops: category→app_details, keyword→app_details, app→reviews)

   applied in app-details-scraper and category-scraper before DB insert

   rankings, and category pages. Green <24h, amber 24-72h, red >72h.

    return identical "Invalid email or password" message.

Fallback/Secondary Scraping Methods for All 11 Platforms
==========================================================

Every platform module now has transparent fallback scraping via withFallback() utility.
Primary method fails → fallback kicks in automatically. Zero overhead on success path.

Architecture:
- withFallback<T>(primary, fallback, context) — try/catch with logging
- FORCE_FALLBACK=true env var to skip primary and test fallback path directly
- --force-fallback CLI flag, --fallback smoke test mode
- BrowserClient always created (lazy — browser only launches if fallback triggers)
- registry.ts passes both httpClient and browserClient to all 11 modules

Per-Platform Fallback Strategies:
- Shopify, Wix: HTTP → Browser (same parsers)
- Zoho: HTTP↔Browser (direction depends on page type)
- Google Workspace: Browser re-launch with fresh context
- Canva: Browser → HTTP bulk page (/apps embedded JSON + text search)
- HubSpot: CHIRP HTTP → Browser page.evaluate() calling CHIRP from browser context
- WordPress, Atlassian, Zoom: REST API → Browser + new HTML parsers
- Zendesk: Browser (Cloudflare) → Algolia search by numeric ID
- Salesforce: Browser SPA → Search API card data

New Files:
- apps/scraper/src/utils/with-fallback.ts (+ tests)
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/parsers/html-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/wordpress/parsers/html-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/zoom/parsers/html-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/zendesk/parsers/algolia-app-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/salesforce/parsers/search-app-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/canva/parsers/bulk-search.ts

Fallback Unit Tests (15 test files, 1062 total tests):
- Every platform has __tests__/fallback.test.ts covering primary success, fallback trigger, both-fail propagation
- Google Workspace: mock browser internals injected, closeBrowser spy for reset behavior
- Canva: tests fallback components directly (searchBulkApps, cached paths, HTTP fallback logic) — cannot mock private methods through module due to vitest ESM isolation
- Zendesk HTML parser tests: parseCategoryHtml, parseSearchHtml with Cheerio extraction
- Test files: shopify, salesforce, canva, wix, wordpress, google-workspace, atlassian, zoom, zoho, zendesk, hubspot fallback.test.ts + parser-specific tests

Smoke Test --compare Mode:
- ./scripts/smoke-test.sh --compare runs primary THEN fallback sequentially
- Shows "PHASE 1: PRIMARY" and "PHASE 2: FALLBACK" headers
- Displays "COMPARE SUMMARY" with pass/fail for each mode
- Can combine with --platform: ./scripts/smoke-test.sh --platform shopify --compare

Production smoke test fix:
- Dockerfile.api now includes scraper build (smoke tests spawn CLI from API container)
- resolveScraperCommand() detects dev (tsx) vs production (node dist/cli.js)
- browser-client.ts uses dynamic import("playwright") so HTTP-only platforms work without Playwright
- Fixed double-counting bug in SSE smoke test endpoint (error+close both firing)

Zendesk Marketplace — 10th Platform Integration
=================================================

Platform ID: "zendesk", Color: #03363D (Zendesk dark teal)
URL: https://www.zendesk.com/marketplace

Architecture:
- Categories & search: Algolia API (direct HTTP, no browser needed)
  - Algolia App ID: 7Z3RM3E33J, Index: appsIndex
  - Requires Referer: https://www.zendesk.com/ header
- App detail pages & featured sections: BrowserClient/Playwright (Cloudflare blocks HTTP)
- Slug format: {numericId}--{text-slug} (e.g., 972305--slack)
- Product type (support/chat/sell) stored in externalId for URL reconstruction
- App URL: /marketplace/apps/{product}/{numericId}/{text-slug}/
- Category URL: /marketplace/apps/?categories.name={Display+Name}
- 16 flat categories, no hierarchy
- hasReviews: true, hasFeaturedSections: true, hasPricing: true, hasLaunchedDate: true

Files created:
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/zendesk/ (urls.ts, constants.ts, index.ts, parsers/)
  - parsers: app-parser.ts, category-parser.ts, search-parser.ts, review-parser.ts, featured-parser.ts
- packages/db/src/migrations/0083_seed_zendesk_platform.sql
- packages/db/src/migrations/0084_seed_zendesk_categories.sql

Files modified:
- packages/shared/src/constants/platforms.ts (PLATFORMS, buildExternalAppUrl, buildExternalCategoryUrl)
- apps/dashboard/src/lib/platform-urls.ts (3 URL builder functions)
- packages/shared/src/similarity.ts (weights, stop words, extractCategorySlugsFromPlatformData)
- apps/dashboard/src/lib/metadata-limits.ts (zendeskLimits)
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/registry.ts (ZendeskModule import + switch case)
- apps/scraper/src/scheduler.ts (5 cron jobs for zendesk)
- apps/scraper/src/process-job.ts (BrowserClient creation condition)

Auto-Include App Categories in "My Categories"
================================================

The starred-categories API endpoint now auto-detects categories from tracked/competitor apps
via appCategoryRankings. Categories are merged with manually starred ones, each tagged with
a `source` field: "starred" (manual only), "auto" (detected only), or "both".

API changes:
- Removed early return when no starred categories exist
- Added platform filter to tracked/competitor app queries
- Query appCategoryRankings with selectDistinctOn to find categories where tracked apps appear
- Merge starred + auto-detected with deduplication, return `source` field

Dashboard changes:
- Section renamed "Starred Categories" → "My Categories" (Folder icon instead of Star)
- Source indicators: Star icon for starred, "Auto" badge for auto-detected
- X (unstar) button hidden for auto-only categories
- Unstarring a "both" category re-fetches to show it as "auto"
- starredSlugs filters to "starred"/"both" only (controls star icon in tree/flat table)
- Updated empty states and confirm modal text
- Overview page: title and empty state updated

Zoom App Marketplace — 8th Platform Integration
================================================

Added Zoom App Marketplace (marketplace.zoom.us) as the 8th platform. Uses public JSON API
exclusively — no HTML scraping or Playwright needed, HttpClient only.

Key characteristics:
- App IDs are base64-like strings (e.g. VG_p3Bb_TwWe_bgZmPUaXw), used as slugs
- App detail API (/api/v1/apps/{id}) requires auth → use filter/search endpoint data
- Individual reviews require auth → hasReviews: false
- Pricing requires auth → hasPricing: false
- 48 selectable categories (flat, no hierarchy)
- 9 curated/featured collections via /api/v1/curatedCategory/preview/excludeBanner
- 5-star rating system, ratings available from filter/search endpoints
- Badges: fedramp_authorized (FedRAMP), essential_app (Essential App)

API endpoints:
- GET /api/v1/apps/filter?category={slug}&pageNum=N&pageSize=100 — category scraping
- GET /api/v1/apps/search?q={keyword}&pageNum=N&pageSize=100 — keyword search
- GET /api/v1/curatedCategory/preview/excludeBanner — all featured sections (single call)
- GET /api/v1/app_categories — category list

Atlassian Category Fix — Correct Slugs, Names, Ordered Parsing
================================================================

Fixed Atlassian categories: replaced 19 incorrect seed categories with the 10 official
ones from marketplace.atlassian.com/categories. The old slugs (charts-diagramming,
cloud-security, code-quality, etc.) were API v1 categories, not the current website ones.

Correct categories: project-management, admin-tools, content-communication, data-analytics,
software-development, it-support-service, design-diagramming, security-compliance,
hr-team-building, sales-customer-relations.

REST API v2 does NOT support category filtering (category/categories/tag params all ignored,
always returns all 5276+ cloud apps regardless). HTML pagination is SPA-only (client-side
GraphQL, ?page=N doesn't change server-rendered data). So category scraping uses HTML
page 1 only (~18 apps per category).

Category parser rewritten to use ordered edges from ROOT_QUERY.marketplaceCategory query
instead of unordered AppTile scan. Now extracts pageInfo (totalCount, hasNextPage, totalPages)
and proper category name from MarketplaceStoreCategoryResponse.

Migration 0075 deletes 17 old wrong categories and upserts the 10 correct ones with proper
names (e.g. "Design and diagramming" not "Design Tools").

Files changed:
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/constants.ts — 10 correct seed categories
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/parsers/category-parser.ts — ordered edges + pageInfo
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/index.ts — HTML fetch with proper page param
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/urls.ts — removed unused apiCategory URL
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/parsers/api-parser.ts — removed unused parseCategoryResults
- packages/db/src/migrations/0075_fix_atlassian_categories.sql — replace wrong categories

Atlassian Marketplace Integration
===================================

Added Atlassian Marketplace as the 7th platform.
Platform ID: atlassian, brand color: #0052CC.

Hybrid approach: REST API v2 for app details/search/reviews/featured + HTML scraping
(window.__INITIAL_STATE__ Apollo cache) for category pages. No browser/Playwright needed.

App identifier: addonKey (e.g. com.onresolve.jira.groovy.groovyrunner) stored as slug.

Post-integration fixes:
- External app URL fix: Atlassian URLs need numeric addonId (not addonKey slug).
  Added `external_id` column to apps table (migration 0074), stored numeric ID from
  both category parser (Apollo cache AppTile.addonId) and app-details scraper
  (REST API json.id). Updated buildExternalAppUrl() with optional 3rd param `externalId`.
  All dashboard components pass app.externalId to external link buttons.
- 4-star rating system: Atlassian uses 4-star ratings (not 5). Added `maxRatingStars`
  to all platform configs (4 for atlassian, 5 for all others). Updated layout.tsx
  rating card, reviews page distribution, Review Pulse card, and inline review stars
  to use dynamic star count from platform config.
- Documented both patterns in files/ADDING_NEW_PLATFORM.md (externalId pitfall,
  maxRatingStars capability).

Phase 0 — Discovery script:
- apps/scraper/scripts/atlassian-explore.ts — enumerate categories, test API, validate featured

Phase 1 — Platform config:
- PLATFORMS entry: hasKeywordSearch, hasReviews, hasFeaturedSections = true; pageSize = 50
- Similarity weights: category 0.35, feature 0.0, keyword 0.30, text 0.35
- Stop words: atlassian, jira, confluence, bitbucket, marketplace, plugin, addon, cloud, server, datacenter
- Metadata limits: appName 50, subtitle 80 (tagLine), introduction 150 (summary), details 5000
- URL builders for app, category, search in shared + dashboard
- Field labels: "Tag Line" (subtitle), "Summary" (introduction), "Description" (details)

Phase 2 — Database:
- Migration 0072: seed account_platforms + platform_visibility (hidden by default)
- Migration 0073: seed 19 flat categories (admin-tools, charts-diagramming, cloud-security, etc.)

Phase 3 — Scraper module (apps/scraper/src/platforms/atlassian/):
- constants.ts: 19 seed categories, scoring config, featured section definitions
- urls.ts: human URLs + REST API v2 endpoints
- parsers/api-parser.ts: parseAddonDetails() + parseSearchResults() from JSON
- parsers/category-parser.ts: extract apps from window.__INITIAL_STATE__ Apollo cache
- parsers/review-parser.ts: parse reviews from REST API JSON
- parsers/featured-parser.ts: parse Spotlight/Bestseller/Rising Star collections
- index.ts: AtlassianModule (HttpClient only, no BrowserClient)
- Registry updated with case "atlassian"

Phase 4 — API:
- Live search via GET /rest/2/addons?text={keyword}&limit=10

Phase 5 — Dashboard:
- VALID_PLATFORMS updated in auth-context, proxy, admin-scraper-trigger
- Sidebar: label "Atlassian", color #0052CC, regex patterns updated
- Badges: "Cloud Fortified" (shield), "Top Vendor" (star)
- Overview cards, platform colors, brand config all updated
- Field labels: Tag Line, Summary, Description

Phase 6 — Scheduler:
- category: daily 06:30
- app_details: 07:00/19:00
- keyword_search: 07:30/19:30
- reviews: daily 10:00
- compute_app_scores: daily 12:30

Risk: REST API v2 deprecated Jan 2026, removal after June 2026.
Mitigation: modular parser architecture, category already uses HTML scraping,
Algolia keys embedded in HTML as potential search fallback.

==========================================

Slug format: {name}--{id} (same -- separator as Canva).

- URL builders in shared + dashboard (app, category, search)

- urls.ts, constants.ts (rate limit 3-5s, 14 seed categories from live sidebar)
- 4 parsers (app, category, search, review) + extract-embedded-data.ts utility
- PRIMARY DATA SOURCE: AF_initDataCallback embedded JSON (ds:1 for app/category/search, ds:6 for reviews)
  Each app entry is a 35-field array: [0]=appId, [3]=[name,shortDesc,detailedDesc,iconUrl,bannerUrl,slug],
  [4]=[developerName,website], [5]=[reviewCount,rating,installDisplay,exactInstalls], [8]=[email,terms,privacy,support,homepage]
- DOM FALLBACK selectors: span.BfHp9b (name), div.kmwdk (shortDesc), pre.nGA4ed (detailedDesc),
  img.TS9dEf (icon), img.ec1OGc (screenshots), div.ftijEf (reviews), span.P0vMD (pricing),
  a.G3sBi.Qh16y (active category), div[data-card-index] (card containers on list pages)
- waitForAngularRender: waits for div.oPwrAb or div[data-card-index] or app links (not app-root)
- Registered in registry.ts, BrowserClient in process-job.ts + cli.ts
- Backfill categories regex added

Phase 4 — API routes:
- live-search: database fallback search (no public API)
- apps: developerWebsite path for developer extraction

Fix Salesforce category tree — flat → hierarchical
====================================================

Salesforce categories were all stored with parentSlug=null and depth=0 in DB,
causing the dashboard to display them as a flat list instead of a tree.

Root cause: seedCategories was a flat list of all slugs (parents + children mixed)
and maxCategoryDepth was 0, so the crawler never recursed into subcategories.

Fix:
- Added SALESFORCE_CATEGORY_CHILDREN map defining parent→children relationships
- Changed seedCategories to only root categories (Object.keys of the map)
- Changed maxCategoryDepth from 0 to 1 (two-level tree)
- Updated parseCategoryPage() to inject subcategoryLinks from the child map
- After deploy, a category re-scrape is needed to populate correct parentSlug values

Files changed:
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/salesforce/constants.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/salesforce/index.ts

Fix timezone discrepancy in Run History table (PLA-76)
=====================================================

Queued (createdAt) and Started (startedAt) showed a 3-hour offset because:
- `createdAt` used PostgreSQL's `DEFAULT NOW()` which returns Istanbul local time for `timestamp without timezone`
- `startedAt` used JavaScript's `new Date()` which is always UTC
- postgres.js treats `timestamp without timezone` values as UTC when reading back

Fix: Set `connection: { timezone: "UTC" }` on the postgres.js client in `packages/db/src/index.ts`.
This forces PG's `NOW()` to return UTC, making it consistent with JS `new Date()`.

Files changed:
1. packages/db/src/index.ts — added `connection: { timezone: "UTC" }` to postgres client config

Canva compound slugs for sub-categories
=========================================

Sub-categories now use compound slugs: {parent}--{topic} format.
- e.g., "project-management--forms", "text-styling--forms", "ai-generation--ai-images"
- Allows shared topics (e.g., "forms") to appear under multiple parents as separate DB records
- Each compound slug is unique per (platform, slug) constraint — no DB migration needed
- External "View on Canva" URLs extract parent from compound slug for correct linking
- Cleanup script deleted 39 old simple-slug sub-category records

Key changes:
1. category-parser.ts: hub pages generate compound slugs in subcategoryLinks, listing pages extract topic from compound slug
2. Added marketplace_topic.forms to text-styling in CATEGORY_TOPIC_MAP (shared topic)
3. platforms.ts + platform-urls.ts: buildExternalCategoryUrl extracts parent from compound slug
4. Tests updated for compound slug format + shared topic coverage


Canva categories restructured to two-level hierarchy (PLA-70)
==============================================================

Previously, Canva used 10 flat "filter categories" (e.g., "Project Management") that grouped
all apps by their marketplace_topic.* tags. Apps were ranked directly under these broad filters.

Now restructured to a two-level hierarchy:
- 10 hub categories (filter categories) — isListingPage: false, no rankings
- ~35 listing sub-categories (topic-level) — isListingPage: true, with rankings

Key changes:
1. constants.ts: maxCategoryDepth 0→1, added CANVA_SUBCATEGORY_LABELS (35 topic display names)
2. category-parser.ts: hub pages return appCount: null, subcategoryLinks; listing pages filter by exact topic tag
3. category-scraper.ts: crawlCategoryGeneric now computes isListingPage from appCount, skips rankings/ads/pagination for hubs
4. categories.ts API: descendant query uses (slug LIKE 'parent-%' OR parentSlug = 'parent') + platform filter

No migration needed — upsert logic naturally updates existing filter categories and creates new sub-categories.


Canva keyword search — real API integration
=============================================

Discovery: Canva has a real search API at POST /_ajax/appsearch/search
- Backed by Elasticsearch, returns exact rankings as shown to users
- Auto-suggestions via POST /_ajax/appsearch/suggest
- Both APIs are behind Cloudflare — need browser context + cf_clearance cookie
- API is public (no Canva login needed), but requires Cloudflare clearance

How it works:
1. Chrome browser launches with saved auth state (cf_clearance cookie)
2. Navigates to /apps to pass Cloudflare
3. Types keyword in search box → triggers Canva's JS to call search API
4. Intercepts all /_ajax/appsearch/search responses
5. Merges all paginated results (100 per page, cursor-based)
6. Returns exact Elasticsearch-ranked results

Search API format:
  Request: POST /_ajax/appsearch/search
    {"A":"UAAAAAAAAAA","B":"BAAAAAAAAAA","C":"keyword","D":{"D":true},"G":100}
  Response: {"A":343,"B":"cursor...","C":[{"A":"appId","B":"name","C":"desc","D":"iconUrl"}]}

Auth state management:
- canva-auth-state.json stores cf_clearance + other cookies
- Generated by scripts/canva-auth.ts (launches real Chrome profile)
- cf_clearance expires periodically — needs refresh via canva-auth.ts script
- Without valid cookies, search returns 0 results

Verified accuracy: "form" keyword → Jotform at #7, Jotform AI Chatbot at #287
(exactly matches what users see on canva.com/your-apps?q=form)

Files changed:
  - apps/scraper/src/platforms/canva/parsers/search-parser.ts (rewritten — parses API JSON)
  - apps/scraper/src/platforms/canva/parsers/suggest-parser.ts (rewritten — parses suggest API JSON)
  - apps/scraper/src/platforms/canva/index.ts (rewritten — browser-based API calls)
  - apps/scraper/src/http-client.ts (added fetchRaw for POST requests)
  - apps/scraper/src/scrapers/keyword-scraper.ts (browser cleanup after scraping)
  - apps/scraper/scripts/canva-auth.ts (auth state capture script)
  - apps/scraper/canva-auth-state.json (saved Cloudflare cookies)

Fix Salesforce category slug format — kebab-case → camelCase (PLA-65)
=====================================================================

- Problem: Salesforce categories may have been stored with kebab-case slugs (e.g. `data-management`) before PLA-62 fixed the format to camelCase (`dataManagement`). This causes data fragmentation across rankings, scores, and snapshots.
- Added `DELETE /system-admin/categories/:slug?platform=` endpoint — deletes a category and all related data (account_starred_categories, category_ad_sightings, category_snapshots, app_category_rankings, app_power_scores) in FK order, returns deleted counts
- Added `POST /system-admin/categories/fix-slugs?platform=` endpoint — finds all categories with kebab-case slugs, converts to camelCase. If camelCase version exists: merges FK references + string references then deletes kebab row. If not: renames slug in-place across all tables.
- `kebabToCamelCase()` helper: converts `data-management` → `dataManagement` via regex
- Both endpoints handle FK-referenced tables (categoryId) and string-referenced tables (categorySlug) separately

Fix Salesforce category mapping with camelCase slug fallback (PLA-62)
=====================================================================

- Problem: category matching relied solely on title-to-title lookup (case-insensitive). If category titles from the AppExchange API didn't exactly match DB titles (e.g., "IT & Administration" vs "It And Administration"), mapping silently failed.
- Fix: added `titleToCamelCase()` utility that converts titles to camelCase slugs (e.g., "Customer Service" → "customerService", "IT & Administration" → "itAndAdministration")
- Enhanced `app-details-scraper.ts` category resolution: tries title match first, falls back to camelCase slug match
- Added `log.warn("unresolved category", ...)` when neither match succeeds — previously silent failure
- Tested: Customer Service, Agent Productivity, Data Management, IT & Administration, Human Resources, Case Management, Field Service all map correctly

API Endpoint Platform Filtering — Comprehensive Sweep
=====================================================
Problem: API endpoints using app slug lookups (eq(apps.slug, slug)) returned apps from any platform.
On Salesforce keyword pages, Ad History showed Shopify apps. Bulk POST endpoints also lacked platform filtering.

Fix (keywords.ts):
- /:slug/ads — added eq(apps.platform, platform) to ad sightings query
- /:slug/rankings — added platform to app slug lookup and rankings query

Fix (apps.ts — 18 endpoints):
- All /:slug/* GET endpoints now use and(eq(apps.slug, slug), eq(apps.platform, platform)):
  rankings, membership, history, reviews, changes, similar-apps, ad-sightings,
  category-ad-sightings, featured-placements, scores, scores/history
- All bulk POST endpoints now filter by platform:
  /categories, /last-changes, /min-paid-prices, /launched-dates, /reverse-similar-counts,
  /featured-section-counts, /ad-keyword-counts, /review-velocity
- /review-velocity raw SQL: added AND a.platform = ${platform}

Dashboard Scraper Trigger Platform Support
==========================================
Problem: Scraper jobs triggered from dashboard UI didn't include platform, defaulting to Shopify.

Fix (admin-scraper-trigger.tsx):
- Extracts platform from URL pathname using usePathname()
- VALID_PLATFORMS set validates extracted segment
- Sends platform in request body when triggering scraper

Fix (system-admin/scraper/page.tsx):
- Added platform selector dropdown (triggerPlatform state, defaults to "shopify")
- Uses PLATFORMS constant from @appranks/shared for dropdown options
- Sends platform in triggerScraper() request body

---

Worker Dual-Queue Fix — Interactive Jobs Not Processing
======================================================
Problem: User-triggered scraper jobs (keyword_search, etc.) enqueued to interactive queue
but worker.ts only listened to background queue. Jobs stayed in "waiting" state forever.

Root cause: API routes (account.ts, keywords.ts, research.ts) each create their own
getScraperQueue() connected to INTERACTIVE_QUEUE_NAME. But worker.ts only created
a Worker for BACKGROUND_QUEUE_NAME.

Fix (worker.ts):
- Creates two BullMQ Worker instances: bgWorker (background queue) and intWorker (interactive queue)
- Background worker: concurrency 1, rate limited (1 job per 5s)
- Interactive worker: concurrency 1, no rate limit (immediate processing)
- Both share error/failure logging with queue name prefix
- Graceful shutdown closes both workers

App similarity scores — multi-dimensional scoring:
- New DB table: app_similarity_scores (appSlugA, appSlugB, overallScore, categoryScore, featureScore, keywordScore, textScore, computedAt)
- Canonical ordering: appSlugA < appSlugB, unique index on (appSlugA, appSlugB)
- Jaccard index for each dimension: category slug overlap, feature_handle overlap, keyword ranking overlap, tokenized text overlap
- Text similarity: name + subtitle + appIntroduction, tokenized with stop words removed (English + Shopify-specific)
- Weighted average: 25% each for category, feature, keyword, text
- Pre-computed via compute_similarity_scores job (same pattern as compute_review_metrics)
- Job collects all unique (trackedApp, competitor) pairs across accounts, batch-fetches data, computes in memory
- API: competitors endpoint enriched with similarityScore { overall, category, feature, keyword, text }
- Dashboard: Similarity column on competitors table with progress bar + percentage, color-coded (red >=70%, amber 40-69%, green <40%)
- Tooltip shows 4 component breakdowns, sortable, toggleable column
- Admin scraper page: manual trigger for compute_similarity_scores job

Keyword grouping (PLA-11):
- Pure frontend feature, no API/DB changes
- New utility: lib/keyword-word-groups.ts — extractWordGroups() splits keywords into words, counts frequency (min 2), filters stop words (a/the/for/app/apps etc.), returns sorted by count desc then alphabetically
- filterKeywordsByWord() uses whole-word matching (not substring) to avoid "ai" matching "email"
- Words deduplicated within a single keyword, case-insensitive, min 2 chars
- New component: KeywordWordGroupFilter — visually distinct from tags: dashed border, rounded-md (not pill), monochrome (no colors), count badge suffix, "Common words:" label
- Single-select toggle (vs tags' multi-select), AND logic with tag filter
- Word groups computed from full keyword list (not filtered), so buttons stay stable when tag filter is active
- useEffect clears activeWordFilter if the word disappears from wordGroups after keyword add/remove
- 26 new tests (18 utility + 8 component)

Keyword suggestions from app metadata (PLA-10):
- New shared utility: packages/shared/src/keyword-extraction.ts — pure function, no DB dependency
- N-gram generation: unigrams (4+ chars, not stop word), bigrams (1+ non-stop), trigrams (2+ non-stop)
- 7 weighted fields: name(10), subtitle(5), introduction(4), categories(3), features(2), description(2), categoryFeatures(2)
- Word count multiplier: 1-word=1x, 2-word=2x, 3-word=3x boosts multi-word keywords
- Filters: must appear in primary field (name/subtitle/intro/description), min 2 fields, max 3 words
- Scores accumulate across fields — same keyword in name(10) + subtitle(5) = 15
- Stop words: common English + Shopify-specific (app, store, tool, solution, powerful, easy, etc.)
- API: GET /api/account/tracked-apps/:slug/keyword-suggestions?debug=true&limit=100
- API returns tracked:boolean per keyword (no longer filtered out, shown as "Added" in UI)
- Computed on-demand (not pre-stored), 4 simple indexed queries + in-memory scoring
- Dashboard component: MetadataKeywordSuggestions with prominent/normal modes
- Prominent mode (empty state): auto-opens, larger CTA button, integrated into keywords empty state
- Normal mode: collapsible "Suggest keywords" outline button above keyword table
- UI shows: keyword, source field badges, count × score, Shopify search link, Add/Added state
- Weight legend footer for algorithm transparency during iteration
- 35 new tests (24 extraction algorithm + 11 component)

Keyword loading states & polling (PLA-13):

- When a pending keyword gets latestSnapshot !== null, it moves to resolvedKeywordIds for animation
- Pending state: Skeleton pulse in ranking cells + Skeleton + Loader2 spinner in Total Results cell

- Both suggestion components now parse POST response and forward keywordId/scraperEnqueued to parent

Competitor loading states & polling (PLA-15):
- Same pattern as PLA-13 keywords, applied to competitors page (/apps/[slug]/competitors)
- API: POST competitor endpoint always returns scraperEnqueued=true (enqueues scrape pipeline)
  - Unlike keywords, competitor apps often already have a basic snapshot from search
  - The scrape pipeline (app_details → reviews → compute_review_metrics → compute_similarity_scores) produces enriched data
- Frontend: pendingCompetitorSlugs Map<string, number> (slug → addedAt timestamp) + resolvedCompetitorSlugs Set
- loadCompetitors() accepts silent=true param to skip full table skeleton
- addCompetitor() uses silent load + tracks pending slug when scraperEnqueued=true
- Polling: 5s interval when pendingCompetitorSlugs is non-empty, refreshes competitors + last changes
- Resolution: when reviewVelocity !== null OR similarityScore !== null (enriched data from compute jobs)
  - 120s timeout fallback for edge cases where compute jobs don't produce output
- Skeleton shown only on compute-job cells (similarity, v7d/v30d/v90d, momentum)
- Already-available cells (rating, reviews, pricing, featured, etc.) show actual data immediately
- Loader2 spinner next to app name while pending
- Resolved cells: animate-in fade-in duration-700 animation (2s auto-clear)
- New row: animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-top on the TableRow

Worker re-structure — dual queue architecture (PLA-14):
- Problem: single BullMQ queue (scraper-jobs) with concurrency=1 meant user-triggered jobs waited behind long-running scheduled jobs
- Solution: two separate queues with dedicated workers in separate containers
  - scraper-jobs-interactive: processes user-triggered jobs (track app, track keyword, add competitor) with no rate limiter
  - scraper-jobs-background: processes scheduled/cron jobs, cascade jobs, admin triggers with rate limiter (1 job/5s)
- Shared job processor: process-job.ts extracted from worker.ts, both workers import the same processJob function
- API routing: account.ts routes → interactive queue, scheduler/admin → background queue
- Cascade jobs always go to background queue (not user-blocking)
- System admin scraper page shows per-queue breakdown (interactive/background) with combined totals
- Queue management endpoints (pause/resume/drain/clear) operate on both queues
- Trigger endpoint accepts optional queue parameter (default: background)
- Docker: same Dockerfile.worker image, two services in docker-compose (worker + worker-interactive)
- Files: queue.ts, process-job.ts (new), worker.ts, interactive-worker.ts (new), account.ts, system-admin.ts, admin.ts, scraper page, docker-compose.prod.yml, package.json

Queue tracking in scrape_runs (PLA-17):
- New DB column: scrape_runs.queue (varchar(20), nullable for backward compat)
- Migration: 0036_scrape_runs_queue.sql — simple ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN
- createProcessJob() accepts queueName parameter, workers pass "background" or "interactive"
- All scrape_run inserts include queue: category-scraper (crawl, scrapeSingle), app-details-scraper (scrapeTracked, scrapeApp), review-scraper (scrapeTracked), keyword-scraper (scrapeAll), keyword-suggestion-scraper (scrapeAll), compute-review-metrics, compute-similarity-scores, process-job inline inserts (keyword_search single, keyword_suggestions single, reviews single)
- API: GET /api/system-admin/scraper/runs now supports ?queue=interactive|background filter
- Dashboard Run History table: new "Queue" column with badge (interactive/background), queue filter dropdown alongside type/trigger filters
- Existing runs have queue=null (shown as dash in UI)
- Cascade jobs inherit the originating queue: when app_details runs on interactive queue, its cascade jobs (compute_similarity_scores, reviews, etc.) also go to the interactive queue instead of always defaulting to background
- cascadeOpts computed once from queueName in createProcessJob(), passed to all 7 enqueueScraperJob cascade calls
- Files: scrape-runs.ts, 0036_scrape_runs_queue.sql, process-job.ts, worker.ts, interactive-worker.ts, category-scraper.ts, app-details-scraper.ts, review-scraper.ts, keyword-scraper.ts, keyword-suggestion-scraper.ts, compute-review-metrics.ts, compute-similarity-scores.ts, system-admin.ts (API), scraper/page.tsx, scraper-page.test.tsx
