Keyword opportunity scoring (PLA-25):
- Composite opportunity score (0-100) per keyword computed from keywordSnapshots.results JSONB
- 5 scoring components: Room(35%), Demand(20%), Organic(15%), Maturity(10%), Quality(20%)
  - Room: max(0, min(1, 1 - top8Reviews/20000)) — fewer reviews in top 8 = more room
  - Demand: min(1, totalResults/1000) — more total results = more popular
  - Organic: (24 - sponsoredCount)/24 — fewer ads = more organic opportunity
  - Maturity: 1 - min(1, count1000/12) — fewer 1000+ review apps = less mature market
  - Quality: bfsFactor × ratingFactor — fewer BFS apps and lower top4 rating = quality gap
- Shared utility: packages/shared/src/keyword-opportunity.ts
  - computeKeywordOpportunity(results, totalResults) → KeywordOpportunityMetrics
  - Separates organic vs sponsored/built-in, computes raw stats + scores + topApps info
  - Exported types: KeywordOpportunityMetrics, KeywordOpportunityScores, KeywordOpportunityStats, TopAppInfo
- API: POST /api/keywords/opportunity — bulk endpoint
  - Input: { slugs: string[] } (max 100)
  - Reads latest keywordSnapshot per slug via DISTINCT ON query
  - Returns Record<slug, KeywordOpportunityMetrics>
- Dashboard: Score column in keywords table
  - Color-coded badge: green(≥60), amber(30-59), red(<30)
  - Lazy-loaded via fetchWithAuth after keywords load
  - Sortable by score (sortBySlug="_score")
- KeywordOpportunityPopover component: click score badge to see breakdown
  - 5 component bars with percentage + weight labels
  - First Page Analysis: total results, organic/sponsored count, avg rating, BFS count, 1000+/100+ counts
  - Review Concentration: top 1 share %, top 4 share %
  - Top Apps: top 4 with icon, name, rating, review count, BFS badge
  - Uses Radix Popover from radix-ui package
- 23 unit tests covering scoring components, edge cases, composite scenarios
- No DB changes — all data from existing keywordSnapshots.results JSONB
- Files created: packages/shared/src/keyword-opportunity.ts, apps/dashboard/src/components/keyword-opportunity-popover.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/__tests__/lib/keyword-opportunity.test.ts
- Files modified: packages/shared/src/index.ts, apps/api/src/routes/keywords.ts, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/apps/[slug]/keywords-section.tsx

Competitor suggestions (PLA-12):

  - Response: appSlug, appName, iconUrl, averageRating, ratingCount, pricingHint, isBuiltForShopify, isAlreadyCompetitor, similarity scores, categoryRanks, isShopifySimilar

App Visibility & App Power Scores:
- New DB tables: app_visibility_scores (historical daily per app per category) and app_power_scores (historical daily per app per category)
- Migration: 0039_app_scores.sql — extends scraper_type enum with compute_app_scores, creates both tables with indexes
- Drizzle schema: packages/db/src/schema/app-scores.ts
- Shared scoring functions (pure, no DB dependency):
  - packages/shared/src/app-visibility.ts: page-boundary decay model (24 apps/page, PAGE_DECAY=0.3), rank_weight = (1/log2(rank+1)) * decay^page, visibility_raw = SUM(totalResults * rank_weight)
  - packages/shared/src/app-power.ts: 4-component weighted score — rating(35%), review authority(25%, log scale), category rank(25%, percentile * page_penalty * size_weight), momentum(15%, accMacro normalized)
- Compute job: apps/scraper/src/jobs/compute-app-scores.ts
  - Prerequisite check: requires app_details, keyword_search, reviews, category completed today
  - If not met before 18:00 UTC: re-enqueues with 30min delay; after cutoff: creates failed run
  - Batch SQL queries: latest keyword rankings, totalResults, category ranks, category sizes, app info, momentum
  - Normalizes scores per category (0-100): max visibility/power in each category = 100
  - Idempotent: ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE for re-runs
  - Scheduled daily at 09:00 UTC
- API endpoints:
  - GET /api/apps/:slug/scores — latest visibility + power per category
  - GET /api/apps/:slug/scores/history — historical data with days/category filters
  - GET /api/categories/:slug/scores — leaderboard (sort by visibility or power)
  - GET /api/categories/:slug/scores/history — category-level trends
- Dashboard:
  - App overview page: new "App Scores" card with Visibility (blue) and Power (purple) display per category, showing score 0-100, keyword count, and component breakdown
  - Category page: Vis and Pwr sortable columns in CategoryAppResults table (blue/purple colored)
  - API utility: getAppScores, getAppScoresHistory, getCategoryScores in lib/api.ts
- System Admin: compute_app_scores added to validTypes, SCRAPER_TYPES (cronHours: [9]), runs filter expanded to accept all types

Restructure Visibility (account-scoped) & Power (leaf categories only):
- Visibility scores restructured from per-category to per-account per-tracked-app context
  - Different tracked apps have different keywords, so same competitor gets different visibility scores per context
  - Schema: app_visibility_scores drops categorySlug, adds accountId (FK accounts.id) + trackedAppSlug (FK apps.slug)
  - Unique index: (accountId, trackedAppSlug, appSlug, computedAt)
  - Migration 0040: DROP + CREATE (no production data yet)
- Power scores now computed only for leaf categories (isListingPage=true)
  - Schema unchanged, compute job filters to leaf categories only
- New shared utility: computeWeightedPowerScore(inputs: { powerScore, appCount }[])
  - Weighted average: sum(powerScore_i * appCount_i) / sum(appCount_i) — bigger categories weigh more
- Compute job restructured into two phases:
  - Phase A (Visibility): queries distinct (accountId, trackedAppSlug) from account_tracked_keywords, gets keyword IDs and competitor slugs per context, computes and normalizes visibility within each context
  - Phase B (Power): filters to leaf categories only, rest unchanged
- API changes:
  - GET /api/apps/:slug/scores: returns { visibility: [...by trackedAppSlug], power: [...by categorySlug], weightedPowerScore }
  - GET /api/apps/:slug/scores/history: accepts trackedApp query param for visibility, category for power
  - GET /api/categories/:slug/scores: returns only power scores (no visibility)
  - GET /api/account/competitors: enriched with visibilityScore + weightedPowerScore per competitor
  - GET /api/account/tracked-apps/:slug/competitors: same enrichment, visibility scoped to tracked app
- Dashboard:
  - App overview "App Scores" card: visibility section (per tracked-app context) + power section (per leaf category) + weighted aggregate
  - Competitor tables (per-app + global): new Vis (blue) and Pwr (purple) toggleable/sortable columns
  - Category app table: removed Vis column, kept only Pwr column
- Files modified: packages/db/src/schema/app-scores.ts, packages/shared/src/app-power.ts, packages/shared/src/index.ts, apps/scraper/src/jobs/compute-app-scores.ts, apps/api/src/routes/apps.ts, apps/api/src/routes/categories.ts, apps/api/src/routes/account.ts, apps/dashboard/src/lib/api.ts, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/apps/[slug]/page.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/apps/[slug]/competitors-section.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/competitors/page.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/categories/[slug]/app-results.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/categories/[slug]/page.tsx

Score Breakdown Popovers (Hover):
- Hover-triggered Radix Popover components that explain how each score (Power 0-100, Visibility 0-100) was calculated
- PowerScorePopover: shows 4-component breakdown with ScoreBar visuals — Rating(35%), Review Auth.(25%), Category Rank(25%), Momentum(15%), footer explains normalization
- WeightedPowerPopover: shows per-category list with power score + app count weight + percentage, footer explains weighted average formula
- VisibilityScorePopover: 5-step formula explanation — keyword count, contribution formula, rank weight table (1/log₂(rank+1)), page penalty (70% drop/page), raw score sum
- API enrichment: competitor endpoints now return visibilityKeywordCount, visibilityRaw, powerCategories[] alongside existing visibilityScore and weightedPowerScore
  - Power SQL query updated to JOIN categories table for c.title
  - Visibility query expanded to select keywordCount + visibilityRaw
  - Both global (/account/competitors) and per-app (/account/tracked-apps/:slug/competitors) endpoints enriched
- Integration points:
  - Category page (/categories/[slug]): Pwr column wraps score in PowerScorePopover, page.tsx passes ratingScore/reviewScore/categoryScore/momentumScore maps alongside powerScore
  - App overview (/apps/[slug]): App Scores card wraps each visibility row in VisibilityScorePopover and each power row in PowerScorePopover, entire row is cursor-help clickable
  - Per-app competitors (/apps/[slug]/competitors): Vis column uses VisibilityScorePopover, Pwr column uses WeightedPowerPopover
  - Global competitors (/competitors): same wrapping as per-app
- Visual design: dotted underline on hoverable score values (border-b border-dotted), cursor-help, consistent color coding (green ≥60, amber 30-59, red <30)
- No DB schema changes — all data from existing tables (app_visibility_scores, app_power_scores, categories, category_snapshots)
- Position/totalApps info: app overview shows (#position/totalApps) next to each category title; PowerScorePopover header displays rank context
  - API /api/apps/:slug/scores: enriched with position (from app_category_rankings DISTINCT ON) and totalApps (from category_snapshots) per power entry
  - API /api/categories/:slug/scores: returns totalApps at response level, positions derived from sorted scores
  - Category listing page: passes position + totalApps from score maps to PowerScorePopover
- WeightedPowerPopover redesigned: shows full 4-component breakdown (ScoreBar) per category instead of simple category+score lines
  - Each category shows: title, app count, weight %, overall power score, plus Rating/Review Auth./Category Rank/Momentum bars
  - API: both competitor endpoints enriched with ratingScore, reviewScore, categoryScore, momentumScore per powerCategory entry
  - Scrollable content (max-h-[70vh]) for apps with many categories
- Category Rank formula fix: replaced `percentile * pagePenalty * sizeWeight` with `1/log₂(position+1) * pagePenalty`
  - Old formula: sizeWeight = log10(totalApps+1) inflated scores >1.0, so all page-1 apps showed 100% Category Rank
  - New formula: logarithmic rank decay (same as visibility), score always in [0, 1], meaningful spread within page 1
  - Expected scores: Rank 1→100%, Rank 5→39%, Rank 10→29%, Rank 20→23%, Rank 25 (page 2)→6%
  - Requires compute_app_scores job re-run to update stored values
- Competitor power queries: INNER JOIN with is_listing_page=true to exclude parent categories
- WeightedPowerPopover: shows rank position per category (#N/M apps, X%)
  - API: both competitor endpoints enriched with rank_position via LATERAL join to app_category_rankings
- Column headers: renamed "Vis"→"Visibility" and "Pwr"→"Power" in all table headers
- Power data source fix: compute job query changed from `WHERE is_tracked = true` to `WHERE average_rating IS NOT NULL OR rating_count IS NOT NULL`
  - Previously only tracked apps had rating/review data loaded, so non-tracked apps in a category got ratingScore=0 and reviewScore=0
  - Category scraper already writes averageRating and ratingCount to apps table for ALL apps from listing pages
  - Fix ensures all apps with rating/review data (regardless of tracking status) contribute properly to power score normalization
  - Momentum (accMacro) still only available for tracked/competitor apps — acceptable since review metrics require review scraping
- Rating score formula improved: `rating/5` (linear) → `((rating-3)/2)^1.5` (power curve with floor at 3.0)
  - Old formula: 3.0→60%, 4.0→80%, 5.0→100% — too generous, only 20pp spread in 4.0-5.0 range
  - New formula: 3.0→0%, 4.0→35%, 4.6→72%, 4.8→85%, 5.0→100% — better differentiation where it matters
  - Floor at 3.0 (below 3.0 → 0%), power 1.5 curve rewards high ratings more

- Files modified: packages/shared/src/app-power.ts, apps/api/src/routes/account.ts, apps/api/src/routes/apps.ts, apps/api/src/routes/categories.ts, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/categories/[slug]/page.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/categories/[slug]/app-results.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/apps/[slug]/page.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/apps/[slug]/competitors-section.tsx, apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/competitors/page.tsx

  - Competitors: POST /:id/competitors (add, enqueue scraper if no snapshot), DELETE /:id/competitors/:slug
  - Data endpoint: GET /:id/data — single endpoint returns ALL page data:
    - project, keywords (with totalResults), competitors (enriched with app info, snapshot, power score)
    - keywordRankings matrix (keyword_slug → app_slug → position)
    - competitorSuggestions: apps that rank for project keywords, sorted by matched count
    - keywordSuggestions: from competitor rankings (source A) + metadata extraction (source B), deduplicated
    - wordAnalysis: market language word frequency from extractKeywordsFromAppMetadata across all competitors
    - categories: category landscape with competitor positions from app_category_rankings
    - featureCoverage: feature matrix from app snapshot categories/subcategories, gap detection (<50%)
    - opportunities: keyword opportunity scores using computeKeywordOpportunity from shared
- Snowball suggestion algorithms:
  - Competitor suggestions: query app_keyword_rankings for apps ranking in project keywords, GROUP BY app_slug, enrich with app info + matched keyword names
  - Keyword suggestions: Source A (ranking data) — keywords competitors rank for; Source B (metadata) — extractKeywordsFromAppMetadata per competitor, merge ≥2 apps
  - Word analysis: aggregate extractKeywordsFromAppMetadata across all competitors, filter to ≥2 apps

  - Sidebar: "Research" link with FlaskConical icon from lucide-react

    - Layer 0: empty state with centered keyword input and example text

    - Layer 2: competitor table (rating, reviews, pricing, power, ranking counts) + keyword suggestions
    - Layer 3: market language (tag cloud + table), category landscape, feature coverage (bar chart with gap detection), keyword opportunities table

AI-Powered Virtual App Generation
===================================

Generate 2-4 differentiated virtual app concepts from research competitor data using OpenAI gpt-4o structured output.

Backend (apps/api/src/routes/research.ts):
- POST /:id/virtual-apps/generate — AI generation endpoint
- buildResearchSummary() compresses research data to ~5-8K tokens for the prompt
- OpenAI gpt-4o with structured JSON schema output, temperature 0.8, 120s timeout
- Post-validation: filters features/integrations/languages against known competitor values
- Category validation: matches against known category tree by title/URL slug
- Icon validation: ensures single emoji character with codepoint > 0xFF, fallback to predefined set
- Field truncation: name (30), appCardSubtitle (62), seoTitle (60), seoMetaDescription (160)
- Error handling: 503 (no API key), 400 (< 2 competitors), 429 (rate limit/quota), 502 (AI error)
- createdBy tracking: stores user who triggered generation

Frontend (apps/dashboard):
- "Generate with AI" button with animated purple gradient + shimmer CSS effect
- Full-screen AiGenerationOverlay with 8-step progress animation, floating particles, progress bar
- Redesigned VA cards: icon + name prominent, subtitle, stats row, AI/Manual badge, creator name, hover actions
- Preview page: mock Shopify App Store detail page rendering
- CompetitorCountBadge: reusable component showing how many competitors have each feature/integration
- Feature/Integration/Language pickers: selected items sort to top
- Category slug matching fixed: extracts slugs from VA category URLs for proper tree matching

Database:
- Migration 0055: research_virtual_apps table (CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS)
- Migration 0056: icon + color columns (ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS)
- Migration 0057: generated_by_ai boolean column
- Migration 0058: created_by UUID FK to users table (ON DELETE SET NULL)
- All migrations registered in journal and idempotent for safe production deployment

Dependencies:
- Added openai ^6.27.0 to apps/api
- Requires OPENAI_API_KEY environment variable

## Fix Canva Category Parent-Child Relationships (1-to-N)

Problem:
- Canva subcategories could belong to multiple parent categories (e.g., "forms" is under both "project-management" and "text-styling")
- The old approach created separate rows with compound slugs ("project-management--forms", "text-styling--forms"), causing duplicate data and confusing UX

Solution:
- Created `category_parents` junction table for 1-to-N parent-child relationships
- Migration 0062 backfills junction table from existing parentSlug, merges compound-slug categories into simple slugs, migrates all references (snapshots, rankings, scores, starred, ad sightings), deduplicates, and cleans up orphaned rows
- Canva parser now returns simple slugs (e.g., "forms") with `parentSlug` field instead of compound slugs
- Category scraper upserts junction rows; handles multi-parent by adding additional parent links even when category was already visited
- API routes use junction table for: tree building, children lookup, breadcrumb walking, hub page descendants
- System-admin parentTitle shows comma-separated parent names via junction table
- Dashboard shows multiple parent breadcrumbs for multi-parent categories
- Removed compound-slug formatting logic from platform-urls.ts

Files changed:
- packages/db/src/schema/category-parents.ts (NEW)
- packages/db/src/index.ts
- packages/db/src/migrations/0062_category_parents.sql (NEW)
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/canva/parsers/category-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/platform-module.ts
- apps/scraper/src/scrapers/category-scraper.ts
- apps/api/src/routes/categories.ts
- apps/api/src/routes/system-admin.ts
- apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/[platform]/categories/[slug]/page.tsx
- apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/system-admin/categories/page.tsx

HubSpot App Marketplace — 11th Platform Integration
=====================================================

Platform: hubspot, Color: #FF7A59
Base URL: https://ecosystem.hubspot.com/marketplace
Client: BrowserClient (Playwright) — pure SPA, no SSR/embedded JSON
Capabilities: hasKeywordSearch, hasReviews, hasFeaturedSections, hasPricing = true
            hasLaunchedDate, hasAdTracking, hasSimilarApps, hasAutoSuggestions, hasFeatureTaxonomy = false
Categories: 6 top-level hierarchical (sales, marketing, service, commerce, operations, content)

URL patterns:
- App: /marketplace/listing/{slug}
- Category: /marketplace/apps/{slug} or /marketplace/apps/{parent}/{child}
- Search: /marketplace/explore?query={keyword}
- Featured: /marketplace/featured/{collectionSlug}

Architecture: BrowserClient renders pages → parse rendered DOM with Cheerio.
App parser tries JSON-LD first, then falls back to DOM selectors.
Category/search parsers look for app cards by class patterns, fallback to /marketplace/listing/ links.

New files (7):
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/hubspot/index.ts (PlatformModule)

- apps/scraper/src/platforms/hubspot/parsers/category-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/hubspot/parsers/search-parser.ts
- apps/scraper/src/platforms/hubspot/parsers/review-parser.ts

Live Smoke Test Runner in Scraper Health Dashboard
===================================================

Added an integrated live smoke test feature to the scraper health dashboard
(/system-admin/scraper-health). Replaces manual SSH + smoke-test.sh.

Architecture: SSE (Server-Sent Events)
- GET /api/system-admin/scraper/smoke-test → streams init/start/complete/summary/done events
- POST /api/system-admin/scraper/smoke-test/check → retry a single check (JSON response)
- Uses fetch() + ReadableStream + TextDecoder for SSE with JWT auth headers
- Max 6 concurrent checks, max 2 browser-platform checks at a time

Shared Config (packages/shared/src/constants/smoke-test.ts):
- SmokePlatform, SmokeCheck types
- SMOKE_PLATFORMS array — all 11 platforms with checks/args (mirrors smoke-test.sh)
- SMOKE_CHECKS, BROWSER_PLATFORMS constants
- getSmokeCheck(), getSmokePlatform(), countTotalSmokeChecks() helpers

Frontend:
- useSmokeTest() hook — manages SSE stream, results Map, progress, start/stop/retryCheck
- SmokeTestPanel component — collapsible Card below health matrix:
  - 11×5 matrix (platforms × checks) with animated status cells
  - PENDING (gray dot) → RUNNING (blue pulse + elapsed timer) → PASS (green check) / FAIL (red X)
  - Progress bar with percentage
  - Click failed cell to expand error details + retry button
  - Summary footer with pass/fail/N/A counts + total duration

Files created:
- packages/shared/src/constants/smoke-test.ts
- apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/system-admin/scraper-health/use-smoke-test.ts
- apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/system-admin/scraper-health/smoke-test-panel.tsx
- packages/shared/src/__tests__/smoke-test.test.ts (17 tests)
- apps/api/src/__tests__/routes/smoke-test.test.ts (10 tests)

Files modified:
- packages/shared/src/index.ts (export smoke test types/constants)
- apps/api/src/routes/system-admin.ts (SSE + retry endpoints)
- apps/dashboard/src/app/(dashboard)/system-admin/scraper-health/page.tsx (import SmokeTestPanel)

PLA-179: Global API rate limiting middleware
- Added global onRequest hook in apps/api/src/index.ts (after auth middleware so request.user is available)
- Three-tier rate limiting using existing RateLimiter class:
  - Authenticated users: 200 req/min keyed by userId
  - Unauthenticated/public: 30 req/min keyed by IP
  - System admin endpoints (/api/system-admin/*): 20 req/min keyed by userId
- Health check endpoints (/health, /health/live, /health/ready) and OPTIONS preflight are exempt
- Returns 429 with Retry-After header (seconds) when limit exceeded
- Extended rate-limiter tests: 4 → 9 tests (reset, blocking persistence, retryAfterMs decay, multi-tier independence)
- All 491 API tests passing

## PLA-235: Fix studio draft editor showing empty title and subtitle (2026-03-29)
- `name` and `appCardSubtitle` live on the `apps` table (app root), NOT on `appSnapshots`
- Draft editor's `makeField()` was reading all values from `snapshot`, so title/subtitle were always empty
- Same bug in v2 app page `computeListingHealth()` and `ListingScorecard` component
- Fix: read `name`/`appCardSubtitle` from `app` object, fall back to snapshot for backward compat
- Added `app` prop to `ListingScorecard` component
- 2 new regression tests for ListingScorecard (app prop vs snapshot fallback)

## PLA-1035: Track delisted apps with dedicated state + admin observation page (2026-04-12)
- Added `apps.delisted_at` column + partial index via migration 0141
- `scrapeApp()` in `app-details-scraper.ts` now catches HTTP 404 via `is404Error()` helper, upserts app row with `delisted_at = COALESCE(existing, NOW())`, and throws `AppNotFoundError` — batch callers already count this as processed (not failed), so `items_failed` metric is cleaned up as a side-effect
- Re-listed detection: successful re-scrape clears `delisted_at` back to NULL via the main upsert
- New API endpoints: `GET /api/system-admin/apps/delisted` (platform/search/date filters + pagination) and `POST /api/system-admin/apps/:id/mark-relisted`
- New dashboard page at `/system-admin/delisted-apps` with filter bar + table + "Mark re-listed" action
- Observation phase: delisted apps are still retried each run so the re-listed path stays exercised
- 6 unit tests added for `is404Error` (including AppNotFoundError interop, non-404 HTTP errors, null/undefined safety, no false-positive substring matches)
- Updated `files/ADDING_NEW_PLATFORM.md` Quick Checklist + new "Delisted App Handling" section: HTTP-based platforms auto-work, API-based platforms must throw `AppNotFoundError` explicitly

## PLA-1049: Category scraper refreshes snapshots (2026-04-12)

Insert new snapshot when any drift OR snapshot older than maxAgeMs; emit `appFieldChanges` per drifted field.

## PLA-1048: bulk_via_category scope for app_details (2026-04-12)
- New `AppDetailsScraper.scrapeAllViaCategoryApi`: iterates every category page (seeds + subcategoryLinks up to maxCategoryDepth), dedupes cards (richer card wins on ratingCount), upserts apps, calls shared `upsertSnapshotFromCategoryCard` helper. Tolerates per-category fetch failures; metadata captures categories_fetched/category_failures/snapshots_inserted.
- Helper extracted to `apps/scraper/src/utils/upsert-snapshot-from-card.ts` — CategoryScraper and the new bulk path both delegate.
- Routing: scope union widened in `queue.ts`; `process-job.ts` skips BrowserClient for bulk scope and bumps timeout to JOB_TIMEOUT_APP_DETAILS_ALL_MS.
- Scheduler: `ScraperSchedule.options` field added; `salesforce_app_details_bulk` at `0 3 * * *` runs `app_details` with `scope=bulk_via_category`.
- Concurrency: `appDetailsConcurrencyBulk` (5) + `concurrentSeedCategories` (5 for Salesforce).
- Tests: new `app-details-bulk-via-category.test.ts` (5 cases). Full scraper suite 172 files / 2541 tests green.
- Expected impact: ~13k Salesforce apps refreshed in < 5 min (vs ~24h via scope=all). Trade-off: no fullDescription/highlights/media — those remain in browser-based scope=all (PLA-1051 will make that selective).

## PLA-1051: Selective full-detail enrichment (2026-04-12)
- New scope `all_with_full_details` on `app_details`. New method `AppDetailsScraper.scrapeAllWithFullDetails` runs browser path only for apps matching one of 4 predicates: tracked, new (no snapshot / appDetails empty), stale (snapshot > staleDays old, default 7), or today's weekly cohort (`appId % 7 == day_index`).
- `selectFullDetailCandidates` exposed separately for testability; emits per-bucket breakdown into `scrape_runs.metadata.selection_breakdown = {tracked, new, stale, cohort, total}`.
- `process-job.ts` routes new scope and extends the long-running timeout.
- `queue.ts` scope union widened to include `all_with_full_details`.
- Tests in `app-details-selective.test.ts` (6 cases) cover each predicate independently plus combined breakdown.
- Kept `scope=all` untouched for backwards compatibility; selective path is opt-in via explicit `scope=all_with_full_details` (no cron yet — can be added as a weekly schedule once tuned in prod).

## PLA-1048 followup: Fix false-positive drift in snapshot diff (2026-04-12)
- Production run 1 (job 1275) completed in 25.86s, 5573 apps, 0 failures, 5572 snapshots inserted, 2219 field changes.
- Production run 2 (job 1277, same data) produced 1922 snapshots + 3874 false `averageRating` drifts because Postgres `decimal(3,2)` stores "4.80" while `String(4.8)` produces "4.8".
- Fix in `apps/scraper/src/utils/upsert-snapshot-from-card.ts`:
  - averageRating compared as rounded integers (×100) to two decimal tolerance.
  - pricing: when card.pricingHint is empty/whitespace, treat as "no new info" — keep stored value and skip drift detection for this field.
  - pricing comparison is case-insensitive.
- Two new tests in `category-scraper-refresh.test.ts`: decimal format drift and empty pricing preservation. Full suite 21 refresh/bulk/selective tests green.

## PLA-1048 final validation (2026-04-12 23:11 UTC)

- Three-run table logged in Linear comment on PLA-1048.
- Final throughput: ~4300× faster than scope=all for Salesforce full-catalog refresh. Real catalog size is 5573 apps (not 13k as estimated).

## scope=all parity with Shopify (2026-04-12 late)
- `process-job.ts` — when scope=all, if the platform module's `refreshSnapshotFromCategoryCard === true`, route to `scrapeAllViaCategoryApi` instead of `scrapeAll`. Shopify path unchanged (no flag → stays on per-app HTTP loop, already fast).
- Result: System-admin "Scrape ALL" button now works identically for Shopify and Salesforce without any UI change. Under the hood Salesforce uses the bulk HTTP path; Shopify uses its per-app HTTP path. Both complete well under the timeout.
- Email snapshot tests (6) regenerated — they were failing because stored snapshots contained "Apr 12" and the test clock crossed midnight UTC; unrelated to this change.
